        <tr> 
         <td> <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="_Turkey"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Flag_of_Turkey.svg/23px-Flag_of_Turkey.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Flag_of_Turkey.svg/35px-Flag_of_Turkey.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Flag_of_Turkey.svg/45px-Flag_of_Turkey.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="800">&nbsp;</span>Turkey</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Legal_status_of_psilocybin_mushrooms&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: &nbsp;Turkey">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> </td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td>In Turkey magic mushrooms are treated as psilocybin which is illegal. The sale, growth and possession can lead to prosecution. </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td> <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="_Ukraine"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Flag_of_Ukraine.svg/23px-Flag_of_Ukraine.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Flag_of_Ukraine.svg/35px-Flag_of_Ukraine.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Flag_of_Ukraine.svg/45px-Flag_of_Ukraine.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="800">&nbsp;</span>Ukraine</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Legal_status_of_psilocybin_mushrooms&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: &nbsp;Ukraine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> </td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Illegal (Spores are legal)</td> 
         <td>Psilocybin in any form is illegal. According to the Ukrainian Criminal Code, fetal bodies of fungi containing psilocybin are considered a psychotropic substance, and the dose, which entails criminal liability, is 0.01 g of psilocybin, is about 30-40 g of fresh mushrooms. However, the legislation does not prohibit the sale of mushroom spores for cultivation for the purpose of collecting.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">[76]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td> <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="_United_Kingdom"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span>United Kingdom</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Legal_status_of_psilocybin_mushrooms&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: &nbsp;United Kingdom">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> </td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">illegal</td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td>From 18 July 2005<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">[77]</a></sup> both fresh and "prepared" (that is, dried, cooked or made into a tea) psilocybin mushrooms became illegal in the United Kingdom; fresh mushrooms had previously been widely available, even in shops, but section 21 of the Drugs Act 2005 made fresh psychedelic mushrooms ("fungi containing psilocybin"), a <a href="/wiki/Class_A_drug" class="mw-redirect" title="Class A drug">Class A drug</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">[78]</a></sup> Possession and use of psilocybin and psilocin is prohibited since the 2005 Act, but mushroom spores, which do not contain psilocybin, are not regulated. </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td> <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="_United_States"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1235" data-file-height="650">&nbsp;</span>United States</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Legal_status_of_psilocybin_mushrooms&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: &nbsp;United States">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> </td> 
         <td style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Illegal (decriminalized in Ann Arbor, Michigan, Denver, Colorado, Oakland, California, Santa Cruz, California, use and Washington D.C.), Legal in Oregon for mental health treatment in supervised settings starting 1 February 2021, and decriminalized for recreational use<sup id="cite_ref-IBT_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IBT-11">[11]</a></sup></td> 
         <td style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Illegal (decriminalized in Ann Arbor, Michigan, Denver, Colorado; Oakland, California, Santa Cruz, California, and Washington D.C.), Legal in Oregon for mental health treatment in supervised settings starting 1 February 2021<sup id="cite_ref-IBT_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IBT-11">[11]</a></sup></td> 
         <td style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Illegal (decriminalized in Ann Arbor, Michigan, Denver, Colorado; Oakland, California, Santa Cruz, California, and Washington D.C.), Legal in Oregon for mental health treatment in supervised settings starting 1 February 2021<sup id="cite_ref-IBT_11-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IBT-11">[11]</a></sup></td> 
         <td style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Illegal (Grow kits and spores legal in most states, full cultivation decriminalized in Ann Arbor, Michigan, Denver, Colorado, Santa Cruz, California, and Washington D.C.), Legal in Oregon for mental health treatment in supervised settings starting 1 February 2021<sup id="cite_ref-IBT_11-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IBT-11">[11]</a></sup></td> 
         <td>
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           See also: <a href="/wiki/Psilocybin_decriminalization_in_the_United_States" title="Psilocybin decriminalization in the United States">Psilocybin decriminalization in the United States</a>
          </div> In the United States, possession of psilocybin-containing mushrooms is illegal because they contain the <a href="/wiki/Schedule_I_controlled_substance" class="mw-redirect" title="Schedule I controlled substance">Schedule I drugs</a> psilocin and psilocybin. Spores, which do not contain psychoactive chemicals, are explicitly illegal in <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(U.S._state)" title="Georgia (U.S. state)">Georgia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Idaho" title="Idaho">Idaho</a>, and <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a> (<small><i>unlisted states unverified</i></small>).<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">[79]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">[80]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">[81]</a></sup> In the rest of the country, it is not illegal to just sell the spores, but selling them with the purpose of producing hallucinogenic mushrooms is illegal.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">[82]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">[83]</a></sup> Except for <a href="/wiki/Ornamental_plant" title="Ornamental plant">ornamental</a> purposes, growing, selling or possessing <b><i>Psilocybe</i> spp.</b> and <b><i>Conocybe</i> spp.</b> is prohibited by <a href="/wiki/Louisiana_State_Act_159" title="Louisiana State Act 159">Louisiana State Act 159</a>. The cities of <a href="/wiki/Denver" title="Denver">Denver</a>, <a href="/wiki/Colorado" title="Colorado">Colorado</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">[84]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Oakland,_California" title="Oakland, California">Oakland, California</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">[85]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Santa_Cruz,_California" title="Santa Cruz, California">Santa Cruz</a>, California, and <a href="/wiki/Ann_Arbor,_Michigan" title="Ann Arbor, Michigan">Ann Arbor</a>, Michigan have decriminalized the drug.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">[86]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">[87]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">[88]</a></sup> On 3 November 2020 during 2020 US presidential elections, the state of Oregon voted in an <a href="/wiki/Initiative" title="Initiative">initiative</a> to legalize Psilocybin for mental health treatment at licensed centers and to decriminalize the possession of small amounts of all drugs. The new law will come into effect on 1 February 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-IBT_11-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IBT-11">[11]</a></sup> On the same day <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a> passed an initiative to decriminalize the cultivation and possession of "entheogenic plants and fungi".<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">[89]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">[90]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">[91]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td> <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="_Uruguay"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_Uruguay.svg/23px-Flag_of_Uruguay.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_Uruguay.svg/35px-Flag_of_Uruguay.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_Uruguay.svg/45px-Flag_of_Uruguay.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="945" data-file-height="630">&nbsp;</span>Uruguay</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Legal_status_of_psilocybin_mushrooms&amp;action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: &nbsp;Uruguay">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> </td> 
         <td style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Decriminalized</td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td> 
         <td>In Uruguay, psilocybin and psilocin are mentioned in the federal list of controlled substances,Uruguay was first country in South America in decriminalize possession of all and every drugs.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">[92]</a></sup> According to Decreto N° 403/016, all fungal species of the Psilocybe sp. genus are illegal to sell as a medicinal compound, and other psilocybin-containing fungi genera, such as Copelandia, Pluteus and Conocybe are also mentioned in the document.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">[93]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td> <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="_Vietnam"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Flag_of_Vietnam.svg/23px-Flag_of_Vietnam.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Flag_of_Vietnam.svg/35px-Flag_of_Vietnam.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Flag_of_Vietnam.svg/45px-Flag_of_Vietnam.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span>Vietnam</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Legal_status_of_psilocybin_mushrooms&amp;action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: &nbsp;Vietnam">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> </td> 
         <td style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Illegal (but Unenforced)</td> 
         <td style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Illegal (but Unenforced), Magic mushrooms are sold and supplied openly</td> 
         <td style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Illegal (but Unenforced)</td> 
         <td style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Illegal (but Unenforced) Legal for medical or scientific research</td> 
         <td>In Vietnam, psilocybin and psilocin were added to the list of banned substances in 2018 through Decree 73.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">[94]</a></sup> magic mushrooms for ornamental uses made by people or scientific research made by physicians or psychonauts is fully legal in Vietnam. </td>
        </tr>

         <tr>
          <th scope="row" class="navbox-group" style="text-align:center;;width:1%">Legality of<br> drug use</th>
          <td class="navbox-list navbox-odd hlist" style="text-align:left;border-left-width:2px;border-left-style:solid;width:100%;padding:0px">
           <div style="padding:0em 0.25em"></div>
           <table class="nowraplinks navbox-subgroup" style="border-spacing:0">
            <tbody>
             <tr>
              <th scope="row" class="navbox-group" style="width:1%;text-align:center;">International</th>
              <td class="navbox-list navbox-even" style="text-align:left;border-left-width:2px;border-left-style:solid;width:100%;padding:0px">
               <div style="padding:0em 0.25em"> 
                <ul>
                 <li><a href="/wiki/Single_Convention_on_Narcotic_Drugs" title="Single Convention on Narcotic Drugs">1961 Narcotic Drugs</a></li>
